\item Download page\+: Don\textquotesingle{}t add semicolon unless needed in generated code. Fix \href{https://github.com/PrismJS/prism/issues/273}{\texttt{ \#273}} \mbox{[}\href{https://github.com/PrismJS/prism/commit/5a5eec5}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 5a5eec5}}}\mbox{]}

\item Replace Typeplate with Site\+Point on homepage. Fix \href{https://github.com/PrismJS/prism/issues/774}{\texttt{ \#774}} \mbox{[}\href{https://github.com/PrismJS/prism/commit/0c54308}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 0c54308}}}\mbox{]}
